<td style="text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;background-color:gold"><b>Winner</b></td>
<td style="text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2017 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">2017</a></span></td>
<td style="text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;">Team
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</div></div></th></tr><tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;color:darkslategray; font-size:95%">
* Senior club appearances and goals counted for the domestic league only&#32;and correct as of 16:23, 13 March 2021 (UTC)<br /> National team caps and goals correct as of 21:39, 17 November 2020 (UTC)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Serge David Gnabry</b> (<small>German:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Standard_German" title="Help:IPA/Standard German">[gnabi]</a></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> <small>French:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/French" title="Help:IPA/French">[abi]</a></span>; born 14 July 1995) is a German professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a> for <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> club <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany national team</a>.
</p><p>Gnabry started his career in England with <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a>, making his professional debut in September 2012. He also had a brief spell on <a href="/wiki/Loan_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Loan (association football)">loan</a> with <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a> before moving back to Germany to join <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a> in 2016. In 2017, he signed for Bayern Munich before being loaned to <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">1899 Hoffenheim</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_TSG_1899_Hoffenheim_season" title="201718 TSG 1899 Hoffenheim season">201718 season</a>. In <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="201819 FC Bayern Munich season">201819</a>, his first season with Bayern Munich, he won the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Bundesliga" title="201819 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> title and was named their Player of the Season. The <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="201920 FC Bayern Munich season">following season</a>, Gnabry scored 23 goals as Bayern sealed a <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">continental treble</a> consisting of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Bundesliga" title="201920 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a>, <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_DFB-Pokal" title="201920 DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a> and <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201920 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.
</p><p>After appearing for Germany at various youth levels, Gnabry made his senior international debut in November 2016 in a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a> match against <a href="/wiki/San_Marino_national_football_team" title="San Marino national football team">San Marino</a>. He scored a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick#Association_football" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> in the 80 win.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Gnabry was born in <a href="/wiki/Stuttgart" title="Stuttgart">Stuttgart</a>, Baden-Württemberg,<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> to an Ivorian father and a German mother.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> In his youth, Gnabry was a talented sprinter but ultimately chose football over <a href="/wiki/Track_and_field" title="Track and field">track and field</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-talksport_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-talksport-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arsenal">Arsenal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Arsenal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Gnabry's former club <a href="/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a> agreed to a £100,000 deal with <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> side <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in 2010, but he had to wait until 2011, when he was 16, to join the English side.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
Gnabry officially joined Arsenal for the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Premier_Reserve_League" title="201112 Premier Reserve League">201112 season</a>. He played for the <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C._Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Arsenal F.C. Academy">under-18s</a> for the majority of the season but was then promoted to the reserves after impressive displays.<sup id="cite_ref-2011-12season_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2011-12season-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> By the end of the season, Gnabry had played six games, scoring two goals.<sup id="cite_ref-2011-12season_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2011-12season-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9315:_Development_and_limited_gametime"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201215:_Development_and_limited_gametime">201215: Development and limited gametime</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 201215: Development and limited gametime">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="159" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1030" data-file-height="965" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Serge_Gnabry_Arsenal_Members%27_Day_2015_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gnabry with <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in 2015</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Arsenal_F.C._season" title="201213 Arsenal F.C. season">201213 season</a> started off well for Gnabry after he was called up to the Arsenal first team for a pre-season friendly against <a href="/wiki/1._FC_K%C3%B6ln" title="1. FC Köln">FC Köln</a>. He played 24 minutes after coming on at half-time and was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Marouane_Chamakh" title="Marouane Chamakh">Marouane Chamakh</a> in the 69th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He then made his professional first-team debut for Arsenal on 26 September 2012 against <a href="/wiki/Coventry_City_F.C." title="Coventry City F.C.">Coventry City</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Football_League_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League Cup">League Cup</a> as a 72nd-minute substitute for <a href="/wiki/Alex_Oxlade-Chamberlain" title="Alex Oxlade-Chamberlain">Alex Oxlade-Chamberlain</a> as Arsenal routed Coventry 61.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> On 20 October 2012, he made his Premier League debut in the 10 defeat against <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a> at <a href="/wiki/Carrow_Road" title="Carrow Road">Carrow Road</a>. At 17 years and 98 days, he became Arsenal's second-youngest player in the league's history after <a href="/wiki/Jack_Wilshere" title="Jack Wilshere">Jack Wilshere</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he made his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debut, coming on as a substitute in Arsenal's 20 home loss to <a href="/wiki/FC_Schalke_04" title="FC Schalke 04">Schalke 04</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 25 March 2013, Gnabry scored the only goal in a 10 win over <a href="/wiki/CSKA_Moscow" title="CSKA Moscow"> CSKA Moscow U19s</a> in the quarter-finals of the <a href="/wiki/NextGen_Series" class="mw-redirect" title="NextGen Series">NextGen Series</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He scored a late equaliser against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C._Reserves_and_Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Chelsea F.C. Reserves and Academy">Chelsea U19s</a> to make it 33 in the semi-finals of the same competition, before Arsenal lost 43 in extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> In the following game on 8 April, Gnabry scored a goal against <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C._Reserves_and_Academy" title="Liverpool F.C. Reserves and Academy">Liverpool U21s</a> in an eventual 32 away defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the first game of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Arsenal_F.C._season" title="201314 Arsenal F.C. season">201314 season</a>, Gnabry was included in Arsenal's first-team squad against <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a> and started the game on the bench.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He then made his first start for the club on 22 September 2013 in the Premier League against <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a> after <a href="/wiki/Theo_Walcott" title="Theo Walcott">Theo Walcott</a> was ruled out just before kick-off. He played 73 minutes before being subbed out for <a href="/wiki/Ryo_Miyaichi" title="Ryo Miyaichi">Ryo Miyaichi</a> as Arsenal won the match 31.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first professional goal in the next league match against <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City</a> to lead Arsenal to a 21 victory and leave them top of the Premier League table.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On 26 October, he won a penalty away at <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> in an eventual 20 victory for Arsenal.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Gnabry's impressive start to the season resulted in a nomination for the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Boy_(award)" title="Golden Boy (award)">2013 Golden Boy Award</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and a new five-year contract with Arsenal.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Gnabry went on to make 14 appearances in the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Arsenal_F.C._season" title="201314 Arsenal F.C. season">201314 season</a>, including impressive performances in the FA Cup against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and Coventry,<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> with Gnabry helping Arsenal go on to win the tournament that year, featuring on the bench in the next two games against Liverpool<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> and Everton.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following his breakout season, Gnabry missed most of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Arsenal_F.C._season" title="201415 Arsenal F.C. season">201415 season</a> due to a serious knee injury which kept him away from the first team for over a year.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> However, he captained and played 65 minutes for the <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C._Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Arsenal F.C. Academy">Arsenal U21s</a> as they beat <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United" class="mw-redirect" title="Newcastle United">Newcastle United</a> U21s 21 in February 2015.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loan_to_West_Bromwich_Albion">Loan to West Bromwich Albion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Loan to West Bromwich Albion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 7 August 2015, Gnabry joined <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a> on a season-long <a href="/wiki/Loan_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Loan (association football)">loan</a> to gain first-team experience.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut as a substitute in a 32 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> on 23 August 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> However, he did not make any further league appearances, with manager <a href="/wiki/Tony_Pulis" title="Tony Pulis">Tony Pulis</a> stating in October that Gnabry was "not at the required level" to play for West Brom.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In January, he was recalled from his loan after lacking first-team action at West Brom.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C._season" title="201516 West Bromwich Albion F.C. season">201516 season</a> with a Premier League appearance and two League Cup appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-Serge_Gnabry_»_Club_matches_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Serge_Gnabry_»_Club_matches-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SW_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Werder_Bremen">Werder Bremen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Werder Bremen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 31 August 2016, Gnabry signed for <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> side <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a> for a reported transfer fee of £5&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Arsenal manager <a href="/wiki/Ars%C3%A8ne_Wenger" title="Arsène Wenger">Arsène Wenger</a> had wanted to extend Gnabry's contract at Arsenal before his move, but a lack of first-team opportunities meant that the midfielder sought a move elsewhere.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He scored his first goal for Werder Bremen on 17 September 2016 in a 41 away loss to <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In his single season at the club, he made 27 league appearances scoring 11 goals<sup id="cite_ref-201617_season_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201617_season-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> while Werder Bremen finished 8th in the Bundesliga.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bayern_Munich">Bayern Munich</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Bayern Munich">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loan_to_1899_Hoffenheim">Loan to 1899 Hoffenheim</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Loan to 1899 Hoffenheim">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 11 June 2017, <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> announced the signing of Gnabry on a three-year deal for 8&#160;million after activating a clause in his contract with Werder Bremen.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 14 June 2017, Bayern Munich announced that Serge Gnabry was moving to <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">1899 Hoffenheim</a> on a season-long loan. Gnabry had wished for the move to gain more experience.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first and second league goal in the 40 victory over <a href="/wiki/RB_Leipzig" title="RB Leipzig">RB Leipzig</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> He scored 10 goals in his 22 appearances in the season helping Hoffenheim to finish third in the league table and secured a Champions League spot for the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201819 UEFA Champions League">next season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_TSG_1899_Hoffenheim_season" title="201718 TSG 1899 Hoffenheim season">201718 season</a> with 10 goals in 26 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-201718_season_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201718_season-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> He also made an appearance in the <a href="/wiki/Regionalliga_S%C3%BCdwest" title="Regionalliga Südwest">Regionalliga Südwest</a> for the reserve team.<sup id="cite_ref-201718_season_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201718_season-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9320:_Breakthrough_and_silverware"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201820:_Breakthrough_and_silverware">201820: Breakthrough and silverware</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201820: Breakthrough and silverware">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="222" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1072" data-file-height="1400" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Serge_Gnabry_Training_2019-09-01_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-1_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gnabry training with <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in 2019</div></div></div>
<p>On 2 July 2018, Gnabry was presented as a Bayern Munich player. Gnabry was assigned the jersey number 22.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 1 September, Gnabry made his Bundesliga debut for Bayern Munich in a 30 win at Stuttgart when he came on as a substitute in the 77th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> On 3 November 2018, Gnabry scored his first Bundesliga goal for Bayern Munich in a 11 draw against <a href="/wiki/SC_Freiburg" title="SC Freiburg">Freiburg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On 1 December 2018, Gnabry scored two goals in a 21 win against his former club Werder Bremen.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 2 March 2019, Gnabry scored Bayern Munich's 4000th Bundesliga goal during a 51 win over Gladbach, helping the club become the first team to achieve the milestone.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 5 March 2019, he signed a new contract with Bayern Munich until 2023,<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> and finished the Bundesliga season as Bayern's second top scorer with 10 goals in 30 matches. He won his first Bundesliga title as Bayern finished two points above <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Dortmund</a> with 78 points.
</p><p>On 1 October 2019, Gnabry scored four goals in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201920 UEFA Champions League">201920 UEFA Champions League</a> 72 away win against Tottenham Hotspur.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> On 25 February 2020, he scored a brace against Chelsea in the first leg of the Champions League round of 16 in a 30 away win. This made him the first player to score six away goals in London in a single edition of the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> On 14 August, he scored one goal in an <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona_2%E2%80%938_FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Barcelona 28 FC Bayern Munich">82</a> win against <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> in the quarter-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> On 19 August, he scored a brace in a 30 win over <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a> in the semi-finals; hence, he has scored nine goals in nine matches in the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Bayern won 10 over <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2020 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a>, to be his first Champions League title along with his teammate <a href="/wiki/Joshua_Kimmich" title="Joshua Kimmich">Joshua Kimmich</a>, another VfB Stuttgart academy product.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="202021_season">202021 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 202021 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Gnabry started the 202021 season by acquiring the No. 7 shirt, after <a href="/wiki/Franck_Rib%C3%A9ry" title="Franck Ribéry">Franck Ribéry</a> who had worn it for eleven years.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> In the first match of the season, Gnabry scored a hat-trick in an 80 win over Schalke,<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> to be his first ever Bundesliga hat-trick.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth_teams">Youth teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Youth teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Gnabry represented <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> at various <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_youth_football_team" title="Germany national youth football team">youth levels</a>, including under-16, under-17 and under-18 levels.<sup id="cite_ref-talksport_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-talksport-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> In 2017 he was part of the <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_under-21_football_team" title="Germany national under-21 football team">U21 team</a> which won the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2017 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">European Under-21 Championship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-u21euro2017_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-u21euro2017-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2016_Summer_Olympics">2016 Summer Olympics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2016 Summer Olympics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball,_M%C3%A4nner,_L%C3%A4nderspiel,_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball%2C_M%C3%A4nner%2C_L%C3%A4nderspiel%2C_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg/170px-2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball%2C_M%C3%A4nner%2C_L%C3%A4nderspiel%2C_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball%2C_M%C3%A4nner%2C_L%C3%A4nderspiel%2C_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg/255px-2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball%2C_M%C3%A4nner%2C_L%C3%A4nderspiel%2C_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball%2C_M%C3%A4nner%2C_L%C3%A4nderspiel%2C_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg/340px-2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball%2C_M%C3%A4nner%2C_L%C3%A4nderspiel%2C_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2583" data-file-height="3874" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2019-06-11_Fu%C3%9Fball,_M%C3%A4nner,_L%C3%A4nderspiel,_Deutschland-Estland_StP_2220_LR10_by_Stepro.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gnabry playing for <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> in 2019</div></div></div>
<p>On 15 July 2016, <a href="/wiki/Germany_Olympic_football_team" title="Germany Olympic football team">Germany</a> selected Gnabry to participate in the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2016 Summer Olympics  Men&#39;s tournament">2016 Summer Olympics</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 4 August, he started for Germany against <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_under-23_football_team" title="Mexico national under-23 football team">Mexico</a> and scored Germany's first goal after 58 minutes in a 22 draw with Mexico.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he tripled his tally by putting two past <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_under-23_football_team" title="South Korea national under-23 football team">South Korea</a>, the second being a stoppage time free kick that helped Germany salvage a point in a 33 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> On 10 August, Gnabry contributed two more goals in a 100 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Fiji_national_under-23_football_team" title="Fiji national under-23 football team">Fiji</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> In Germany's quarter-final match against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_Olympic_football_team" title="Portugal Olympic football team">Portugal</a>, he scored his sixth goal of the tournament just before half-time as Germany prevailed with a 40 win.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> He ended the tournament as the joint top scorer along with his teammate <a href="/wiki/Nils_Petersen" title="Nils Petersen">Nils Petersen</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> helping Germany to win the silver medal.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior_team">Senior team</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Senior team">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 4 November 2016, Gnabry received his first call-up to the German senior team.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> Seven days later, he scored <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">three goals</a> on his debut in a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_C" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification  UEFA Group C">2018 World Cup qualifier</a> against <a href="/wiki/San_Marino_national_football_team" title="San Marino national football team">San Marino</a> in an 80 away win.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> On 9 October 2019, during a 22 friendly international draw with <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>, Gnabry became the fastest player to reach 10 goals for the nation, doing so in his 11th appearance and beating <a href="/wiki/Miroslav_Klose" title="Miroslav Klose">Miroslav Klose</a>'s record by 2 games.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> On 19 November 2019, he scored three goals in the 61 victory against Northern Ireland. It was his second hat-trick in his international career.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Gnabry, who could not join Bayern's academy since it was a two-hour drive from his home in Stuttgart, went to Arsenal when he was only 15. He later battled for fitness and first-team minutes, so he was loaned out to West Bromwich where manager <a href="/wiki/Tony_Pulis" title="Tony Pulis">Tony Pulis</a> mentioned that he wasn't ready for top-flight football,<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> and was not good enough to play at the Hawthorns.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Pulis later commented on him after his good performances with Bayern: "I'm amazed. We had him at West Brom, we took him on loan and we could never get him fit. He even got taken off in an Under-21 game and he went back to Arsenal and they sold him on ... To have him at West Brom and seeing him do what he's done is absolutely amazing."<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Afterwards, he decided to return to Germany to put his career back on track, where <a href="/wiki/Rio_Ferdinand" title="Rio Ferdinand">Rio Ferdinand</a> mentioned: "I saw him in <a href="/wiki/Dubai" title="Dubai">Dubai</a> on the beach, him and [Hector] <a href="/wiki/H%C3%A9ctor_Beller%C3%ADn" title="Héctor Bellerín">Bellerin</a> came and they were just having a bit of time off. He was in a real kind of down, depressive kind of mood. He wasn't playing, he wasn't fancied and he was just talking about 'I'm really going to work hard now, I'm really going to put my effort in, I'm going to train hard etc'. You could see the determination and the desire to actually become a player and what he's done to go and turn his career around the way he has, has been phenomenal. He deserves enormous credit for that because some players would fold under that disappointment of not playing somewhere."<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> His Arsenal manager Arsène Wenger also commented: "Let's not forget Gnabry, I bought him at the age of 15 from Stuttgart and he was injured a lot. He's creative, he can score goals, right-footed, left-footed, good power, good penetration, very, very clever with the timing of his runs", then added, "I had given him out on loan to West Brom and he didn't play a game. He came back, he was injured. We worked very hard with him for six months and he went out with the German national team, under-21's, and Bayern made a deal with Werder Bremen. He wanted to sign in the end, didn't want to extend his contract (with Arsenal) and I was very sad. But we couldn't get over the line with him because I knew he would have a great career. He can be a number nine, a number 10...he's a very intelligent player."<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> Meanwhile, his former Arsenal teammate <a href="/wiki/Lukas_Podolski" title="Lukas Podolski">Lukas Podolski</a> said: "He was unlucky and had a few injuries. He did well in training".<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His Werder Bremen coach <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Nouri" title="Alexander Nouri">Alexander Nouri</a> mentioned: "He was suffering a lot of injuries, so he couldn't consistently work on his physical strength. He wanted to come back as fast as possible". In the meantime, Gnabry improved his ability to score in both feet, where Nouri added: "I remember he often practiced finishing with his left foot after team sessions, he took a lot of balls and was working on his weaker foot  now he's scoring a lot of goals with it". He also became more involved in defensive duties, as Nouri said: "He is lightning quick, a clinical finisher, but he puts a lot of work now into his defense  that was something he was missing before," then he added, "Now he's making these deep runs back to his own box defending. He's capable of doing this work while on the other hand making deep runs in attack. Before he wasn't able to do it because of a lack of strength physically. After a long period with no injuries, he was able to build up that strength  now he's a complete player. He just needs to prove this over a longer period to become a top international star."<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His trademark cooking celebration was inspired by <a href="/wiki/NBA" class="mw-redirect" title="NBA">NBA</a> star <a href="/wiki/James_Harden" title="James Harden">James Harden</a>, he explained it by saying: "There's a video on YouTube where he's cooking after dropping, I think, a buzzer-beater and won the game. So he was cooking, stirring it up, and that's the celebration."<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Serge_Gnabry&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
